<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:paragon.html>paragon</a> (59676)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:paragon.html>paragon</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">comparison</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">parangón</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">paragonare</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">παρακονάω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">parakonáō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I sharpen, whet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">παρά</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pará</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀκόνη</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">akónē</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">whetstone</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂eḱ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sharp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:paragon.html>paragon</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">paragons</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A person of preeminent qualities, who <a href = vnd.unilang:acts.html>acts</a> as a pattern or model for others. <span class="defdate">[from 16th c.]</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">In the novel, <a href = vnd.unilang:constanza.html>Constanza</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:paragon.html>paragon</a></b> of virtue who would never compromise her reputation.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></i> <b>1599–1602</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hamlet" class="extiw" title="w:Hamlet">The <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedie.html>Tragedie</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:hamlet.html>Hamlet</a>, Prince of Denmarke</a>”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. William Shakespeares Comedies, <a href = vnd.unilang:histories.html>Histories</a>, amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedies.html>Tragedies</a>: Published <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>According</a> to the True Originall <a href = vnd.unilang:copies.html>Copies</a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Folio" class="extiw" title="w:First Folio">First Folio</a>), London |  Printed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Jaggard" class="extiw" title="w:William Jaggard">Isaac Iaggard</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Ed[ward] Blount</a>, published 1623, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/606515358">606515358</a></small>, [Act II, scene ii]:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>Man</a>, <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:paragon.html>paragon</a></b> of animals!</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by Emerson and provide title, author’s full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The <a href = vnd.unilang:riches.html>riches</a> of sweet <a href = vnd.unilang:mary.html>Mary</a>'s son, / Boy-rabbi, Israel's <b><a href = vnd.unilang:paragon.html>paragon</a></b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2014</b> October 21,  <a href = vnd.unilang:oliver.html>Oliver</a> Brown,  “Oscar Pistorius jailed for five years – sport afforded no protection against his tragic fallibilities: Bladerunner's punishment for killing Reeva Steenkamp <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> but a frippery when set against the burden that her bereft parents, June and <a href = vnd.unilang:barry.html>Barry</a>, must carry  | print version: No room for sentimentality in this tragedy, 13 September 2014, p. S22 | ”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Daily_Telegraph" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Daily Telegraph">The Daily Telegraph</a> (Sport)</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/worldnews/oscar-pistorius/11089621/Oscar-Pistorius-jailed-for-five-years-sport-afforded-no-protection-against-his-tragic-fallibilities.html">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Yes, there <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> instances of grandstanding and obsessive behaviour, but many <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> concealed at the time to help protect an aggressively peddled narrative of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oscar_Pistorius" class="extiw" title="w:Oscar Pistorius">[<a href = vnd.unilang:oscar.html>Oscar</a>] Pistorius</a> the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:paragon.html>paragon</a></b>, the emblem, the trailblazer.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A companion; a match; an equal. <span class="defdate">[16th–19th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1590-1593</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Philip_Sidney" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Philip Sidney">Philip <a href = vnd.unilang:sidney.html>Sidney</a></a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Countess_of_Pembroke%27s_Arcadia" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Countess of Pembroke | s Arcadia">The Countess of Pembroke's <a href = vnd.unilang:arcadia.html>Arcadia</a></a></i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Philoclea, who indeed <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> no <b><a href = vnd.unilang:paragon.html>paragon</a></b> but her sister</span></div></dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Spenser to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Comparison; competition. <span class="defdate">[16th–17th c.]</span>
<ul><li><b>1590</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edmund_Spenser" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Edmund Spenser">Edmund Spenser</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Faerie_Queene" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Faerie Queene">The Faerie Queene</a></i>, III.ix:

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">typography<span class="ib-comma">,</span> printing<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The size of type between great primer and double pica, standardized as 20-point. <span class="defdate">[from 18th c.]</span></li>
<li>A flawless diamond of at least 100 carats.</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:paragon.html>paragon</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">paragons</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">paragoning</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">paragoned</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To compare; to parallel; to put in rivalry or emulation with.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>Sir</a> Philip <a href = vnd.unilang:sidney.html>Sidney</a> to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li>
<li>To compare with; to equal; to rival.

<li>To serve as a model for; to surpass.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></i> <b>1603–1604</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Othello" class="extiw" title="w:Othello">The <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedie.html>Tragedie</a> of Othello, the Moore of Venice</a>”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. <li>To be equal; to hold comparison.</li></ol>

***paragraaf.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:paragraaf.html>paragraaf</a> (13164)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">paragraphe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">paragraphus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sign for start of a new section of discourse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">παράγραφος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">parágraphos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">παρά</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pará</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">beside</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">γράφω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gráphō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I write</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paragraaf.html>paragraaf</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paragrafen.html>paragrafen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paragraaf.html>paragraafje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">typography</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">section</span>, a subdivision of a <span class="Latn" lang="en">chapter</span>, usually consisting of multiple <span class="Latn" lang="en">paragraph</span>s</li></ol>

***parasiet.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:parasiet.html>parasiet</a> (12279)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">parasite</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">parasitus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">παράσιτος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">parásitos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. First attested in the 16th century. The sense “parasitic organism” <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Semantic_loan" class="extiw" title="w:Semantic loan">semantic loan</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">parasite</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parasiet.html>parasiet</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parasieten.html>parasieten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parasiet.html>parasietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> parasite <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">parasitic organism</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span> <span class="defdate">[from 19th c.]</span>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:luizen.html>Luizen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:vlooien.html>vlooien</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>andere</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vampiers.html>vampiers</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> bloedergerlijke <b><a href = vnd.unilang:parasieten.html>parasieten</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd><i>Lice, flees and other vampires are bloody annoying <b>parasites</b>.</i></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> parasite, someone who relies on others to get <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a> done. <span class="defdate">[from 16th c.]</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">tafelschuimer</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pardonnez.html>pardonnez</a> (101497)</h1><br></body> 
***parel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:parel.html>parel</a> (11244)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">perle</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">peerle</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">paerle</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:parle.html>parle</a></i>, presumably <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">perle</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">perla</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">perla</i>, plausibly a diminutive of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">perna</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clam, pearl</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pearl</i>; alternative derivations from Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">birna</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">beryllus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:beryl.html>beryl</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> lack plausibility; the letter sense <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> apparently popular etymology from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">nonparel</i>, itself from French <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">nonpareille</i>. Its typographic use <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">perle</i>, following the name given by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jean_Jannon" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Jean Jannon">Jean Jannon</a> to the type used in his miniature editions of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vergil" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Vergil">Vergil</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Horace" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Horace">Horace</a>, amp; the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Testament" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:New Testament">New <a href = vnd.unilang:testament.html>Testament</a></a> in the 1620s, which <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> the smallest printed works to his time.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parel.html>parel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parels.html>parels</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parelen.html>parelen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pareltje.html>pareltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A pearl, a precious, round <a href = vnd.unilang:shelly.html>shelly</a> concretion from oysters or other molluscs</li>
<li>Its imitation</li>
<li>Mother of pearl, the natural material pearls are made from</li>
<li>Anything resembling a pearl's irregular ball-shape, notably a drop of liquid</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (One of) the <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> quality, first pick, the cream</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">printing<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The size of type between <a href = vnd.unilang:diamant.html>diamant</a> and nonparel, equated with the English pearl and standardized as 5 point.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">5-point type</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parisienne.html>parisienne</a></span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:parels.html>parels</a> (8269)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parels.html>parels</a></strong>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:parfum.html>parfum</a> (4471)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:parfum.html>parfum</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">parfumer</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parfum.html>parfum</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parfums.html>parfums</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parfum.html>parfumpje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A perfume, a luxury product providing a fragrant scent.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Essence <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rozen.html>rozen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> diverse <a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>andere</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bloemen.html>bloemen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeer.html>zeer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geren.html>gegeerd</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:natuurlijke.html>natuurlijke</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:parfums.html>parfums</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Essence of roses and various others flowers <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> in high demand for natural <b>perfumes</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">reukwerk</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">parfument</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A perfume, a pleasant scent.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:roos.html>roos</a> Friesia <a href = vnd.unilang:verspreidt.html>verspreidt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hemels.html>hemels</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:parfum.html>parfum</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <a href = vnd.unilang:rose.html>rose</a> Friesia gives out a heavenly <b>scent</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***parka.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:parka.html>parka</a> (34796)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>1780, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nenets_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Nenets languages">Tundra Nenets</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="yrk">парка</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aleut_language" class="extiw" title="w:Aleut language">Aleut</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ale"><a href = vnd.unilang:parka.html>parka</a></i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">па́рка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">párka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup> Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Uralic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Uralic">Proto-Uralic</a></span>; see dialectal <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Finnish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Finnish language">Finnish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fi"><a href = vnd.unilang:parka.html>parka</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rag, swaddling <a href = vnd.unilang:clothes.html>clothes</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which may be cognate from Proto-Uralic, or early borrowing from another <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Uralic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Uralic languages">Uralic</a></span> language.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:parka.html>parka</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">parkas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A long jacket with a hood which protects the wearer against rain and wind.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2002</b> January 3,  James Meek,  <cite>London Review of Books</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Basir tended to wear a <a href = vnd.unilang:beige.html>beige</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:suede.html>suede</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:parka.html>parka</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> his shalwar kameez.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li>A hard, full-fat Italian cheese from <a href = vnd.unilang:parma.html>Parma</a>.</li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">parochiaen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">parochianus</i>. ***parochie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:parochie.html>parochie</a> (12833)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">prochie</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">parochia</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">πᾰροικῐ́ᾱ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">paroikíā</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The <i>a</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> usually syncopated in Middle Dutch, but it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> restored and became increasingly common in early modern Dutch due to influence of the Latin term.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parochie.html>parochie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:parochies.html>parochies</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">parochiën</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly Roman Catholicism</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A parish.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:parochie.html>parochie</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:religie.html>religie</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemeenschap.html>gemeenschap</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gelovigen.html>gelovigen</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:katholieke.html>katholieke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kerk.html>kerk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> één <a href = vnd.unilang:kerkgebouw.html>kerkgebouw</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoort.html>hoort</a></li></ol>

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:partij.html>partij</a> (2553)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">partie</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">partie</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:partij.html>partij</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:partijen.html>partijen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:partij.html>partijtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a> (327)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:passen.html>passen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:passen.html>passen</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">passus</i>. Equivalent to a derivation from etymology 2.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_4">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>just</li>
<li>hardly</li>
<li>only, not until, not any sooner
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>Pas</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kamer.html>kamer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:opgeruimd.html>opgeruimd</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:krijg.html>krijg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koekje.html>koekje</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Only</b> when your room <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> cleared up, you'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> get a cookie.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>now ... really
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Da's <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:stoer.html>stoer</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Now</b> that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>really</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:cool.html>cool</a>!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></strong> (<i>used only predicatively</i>, <i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>fitting, having a proper fit, having the correct size and shape
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>Die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schoenen.html>schoenen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Those <a href = vnd.unilang:shoes.html>shoes</a> do not <b>fit well</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_3">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">passus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_11">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:passen.html>passen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pasje.html>pasje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geography</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mountain pass</li>
